3930     // Despite the generic type of Arrays.copyOf, the mirror might be int, int[], etc.
3931     // Bail out if that is so.
3932     // Inline type array may have object field that would require a
3933     // write barrier. Conservatively, go to slow path.
3934     BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
3935     Node* not_objArray = !bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(false, T_OBJECT, false, BarrierSetC2::Parsing) ?
3936         generate_typeArray_guard(klass_node, bailout) : generate_non_objArray_guard(klass_node, bailout);
3937     if (not_objArray != NULL) {
3938       // Improve the klass node's type from the new optimistic assumption:
3939       ciKlass* ak = ciArrayKlass::make(env()->Object_klass());
3940       const Type* akls = TypeKlassPtr::make(TypePtr::NotNull, ak, Type::Offset(0), false);
3941       Node* cast = new CastPPNode(klass_node, akls);
3942       cast->init_req(0, control());
3943       klass_node = _gvn.transform(cast);
3944     }
3945 
3946     Node* original_kls = load_object_klass(original);
3947     // ArrayCopyNode:Ideal may transform the ArrayCopyNode to
3948     // loads/stores but it is legal only if we're sure the
3949     // Arrays.copyOf would succeed. So we need all input arguments
3950     // to the copyOf to be validated, including that the copy to the
3951     // new array won't trigger an ArrayStoreException. That subtype
3952     // check can be optimized if we know something on the type of
3953     // the input array from type speculation.
3954     if (_gvn.type(klass_node)->singleton() && !stopped()) {
3955       ciKlass* subk   = _gvn.type(original_kls)->is_klassptr()->klass();
3956       ciKlass* superk = _gvn.type(klass_node)->is_klassptr()->klass();
3957 
3958       int test = C->static_subtype_check(superk, subk);
3959       if (test != Compile::SSC_always_true && test != Compile::SSC_always_false) {
3960         const TypeOopPtr* t_original = _gvn.type(original)->is_oopptr();
3961         if (t_original->speculative_type() != NULL) {
3962           original = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(original, t_original->speculative_type(), true);
3963           original_kls = load_object_klass(original);
3964         }
3965       }
3966     }
3967 
3968     if (UseFlatArray) {
3969       // Either both or neither new array klass and original array
3970       // klass must be flattened
3971       Node* is_flat = generate_flatArray_guard(klass_node, NULL);
3972       if (!original_t->is_not_flat()) {
3973         generate_flatArray_guard(original_kls, bailout);
3974       }
3975       if (is_flat != NULL) {
3976         RegionNode* r = new RegionNode(2);
3977         record_for_igvn(r);
3978         r->init_req(1, control());
3979         set_control(is_flat);
3980         if (!original_t->is_not_flat()) {
3981           generate_flatArray_guard(original_kls, r);
3982         }
3983         bailout->add_req(control());
3984         set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
3985       }
3986     }
3987 
3988     // Bail out if either start or end is negative.
3989     generate_negative_guard(start, bailout, &start);
3990     generate_negative_guard(end,   bailout, &end);
3991 
3992     Node* length = end;
3993     if (_gvn.type(start) != TypeInt::ZERO) {
3994       length = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(end, start));
3995     }
3996 
3997     // Bail out if length is negative.
3998     // Without this the new_array would throw
3999     // NegativeArraySizeException but IllegalArgumentException is what
4000     // should be thrown
4001     generate_negative_guard(length, bailout, &length);
4002 
4003     if (bailout->req() > 1) {
4004       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4005       set_control(_gvn.transform(bailout));
4006       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
4007                     Deoptimization::Action_maybe_recompile);
4008     }
4009 
4010     if (!stopped()) {
4011       // How many elements will we copy from the original?
4012       // The answer is MinI(orig_length - start, length).
4013       Node* orig_tail = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(orig_length, start));
4014       Node* moved = generate_min_max(vmIntrinsics::_min, orig_tail, length);
4015 
4016       // Generate a direct call to the right arraycopy function(s).
4017       // We know the copy is disjoint but we might not know if the
4018       // oop stores need checking.
4019       // Extreme case:  Arrays.copyOf((Integer[])x, 10, String[].class).
4020       // This will fail a store-check if x contains any non-nulls.
4021 
4022       bool validated = false;
4023       // Reason_class_check rather than Reason_intrinsic because we
4024       // want to intrinsify even if this traps.
4025       if (!too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_class_check)) {
4026         Node* not_subtype_ctrl = gen_subtype_check(original, klass_node);
4027 
4028         if (not_subtype_ctrl != top()) {
4029           PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4030           set_control(not_subtype_ctrl);
4031           uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_class_check,
4032                         Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
4033           assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
4034         }
4035         validated = true;
4036       }
4037 
4038       if (!stopped()) {
4039         newcopy = new_array(klass_node, length, 0);  // no arguments to push
4040 
4041         ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, original, start, newcopy, intcon(0), moved, true, false,
4042                                                 original_kls, klass_node);
4043         if (!is_copyOfRange) {
4044           ac->set_copyof(validated);
4045         } else {
4046           ac->set_copyofrange(validated);
4047         }
4048         Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
4049         if (n == ac) {
4050           ac->connect_outputs(this);
4051         } else {
4052           assert(validated, "shouldn't transform if all arguments not validated");
4053           set_all_memory(n);
4054         }
4055       }
4056     }
4057   } // original reexecute is set back here
4058 
4059   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4060   if (!stopped()) {
4061     set_result(newcopy);
4062   }
4063   return true;
4064 }
4065 
4066 
4067 //----------------------generate_virtual_guard---------------------------
4068 // Helper for hashCode and clone.  Peeks inside the vtable to avoid a call.
4069 Node* LibraryCallKit::generate_virtual_guard(Node* obj_klass,
4070                                              RegionNode* slow_region) {
4071   ciMethod* method = callee();
4072   int vtable_index = method->vtable_index();
4073   assert(vtable_index >= 0 || vtable_index == Method::nonvirtual_vtable_index,
4074          "bad index %d", vtable_index);
4075   // Get the Method* out of the appropriate vtable entry.
4076   int entry_offset  = in_bytes(Klass::vtable_start_offset()) +
4077                      vtable_index*vtableEntry::size_in_bytes() +
4078                      vtableEntry::method_offset_in_bytes();
4079   Node* entry_addr  = basic_plus_adr(obj_klass, entry_offset);
4080   Node* target_call = make_load(NULL, entry_addr, TypePtr::NOTNULL, T_ADDRESS, MemNode::unordered);
4081 
4082   // Compare the target method with the expected method (e.g., Object.hashCode).
4083   const TypePtr* native_call_addr = TypeMetadataPtr::make(method);
4084 
4085   Node* native_call = makecon(native_call_addr);
4086   Node* chk_native  = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(target_call, native_call));
4087   Node* test_native = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(chk_native, BoolTest::ne));
4088 
4089   return generate_slow_guard(test_native, slow_region);
4090 }
4091 
4092 //-----------------------generate_method_call----------------------------
4093 // Use generate_method_call to make a slow-call to the real
4094 // method if the fast path fails.  An alternative would be to
4095 // use a stub like OptoRuntime::slow_arraycopy_Java.
4096 // This only works for expanding the current library call,
4097 // not another intrinsic.  (E.g., don't use this for making an
4098 // arraycopy call inside of the copyOf intrinsic.)
4099 CallJavaNode*
4100 LibraryCallKit::generate_method_call(vmIntrinsics::ID method_id, bool is_virtual, bool is_static) {
4101   // When compiling the intrinsic method itself, do not use this technique.
4102   guarantee(callee() != C->method(), "cannot make slow-call to self");
4103 
4104   ciMethod* method = callee();
4105   // ensure the JVMS we have will be correct for this call
4106   guarantee(method_id == method->intrinsic_id(), "must match");
4107 
4108   const TypeFunc* tf = TypeFunc::make(method);
4109   CallJavaNode* slow_call;
4110   if (is_static) {
4111     assert(!is_virtual, "");
4112     slow_call = new CallStaticJavaNode(C, tf,
4113                            SharedRuntime::get_resolve_static_call_stub(),
4114                            method, bci());
4115   } else if (is_virtual) {
4116     null_check_receiver();
4117     int vtable_index = Method::invalid_vtable_index;
4118     if (UseInlineCaches) {
4119       // Suppress the vtable call
4120     } else {
4121       // hashCode and clone are not a miranda methods,
4122       // so the vtable index is fixed.
4123       // No need to use the linkResolver to get it.
4124        vtable_index = method->vtable_index();
4125        assert(vtable_index >= 0 || vtable_index == Method::nonvirtual_vtable_index,
4126               "bad index %d", vtable_index);
4127     }
4128     slow_call = new CallDynamicJavaNode(tf,
4129                           SharedRuntime::get_resolve_virtual_call_stub(),
4130                           method, vtable_index, bci());
4131   } else {  // neither virtual nor static:  opt_virtual
4132     null_check_receiver();
4133     slow_call = new CallStaticJavaNode(C, tf,
4134                                 SharedRuntime::get_resolve_opt_virtual_call_stub(),
4135                                 method, bci());
4136     slow_call->set_optimized_virtual(true);
4137   }
4138   if (CallGenerator::is_inlined_method_handle_intrinsic(this->method(), bci(), callee())) {
4139     // To be able to issue a direct call (optimized virtual or virtual)
4140     // and skip a call to MH.linkTo*/invokeBasic adapter, additional information
4141     // about the method being invoked should be attached to the call site to
4142     // make resolution logic work (see SharedRuntime::resolve_{virtual,opt_virtual}_call_C).
4143     slow_call->set_override_symbolic_info(true);
4144   }
4145   set_arguments_for_java_call(slow_call);
4146   set_edges_for_java_call(slow_call);
4147   return slow_call;
4148 }
4149 
4150 
4151 /**
4152  * Build special case code for calls to hashCode on an object. This call may
4153  * be virtual (invokevirtual) or bound (invokespecial). For each case we generate
4154  * slightly different code.
4155  */
4156 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_hashcode(bool is_virtual, bool is_static) {
4157   assert(is_static == callee()->is_static(), "correct intrinsic selection");
4158   assert(!(is_virtual && is_static), "either virtual, special, or static");
4159 
4160   enum { _slow_path = 1, _fast_path, _null_path, PATH_LIMIT };
4161 
4162   RegionNode* result_reg = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
4163   PhiNode*    result_val = new PhiNode(result_reg, TypeInt::INT);
4164   PhiNode*    result_io  = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::ABIO);
4165   PhiNode*    result_mem = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::MEMORY, TypePtr::BOTTOM);
4166   Node* obj = argument(0);
4167 
4168   if (obj->is_InlineType() || gvn().type(obj)->is_inlinetypeptr()) {
4169     return false;
4170   }
4171 
4172   if (!is_static) {
4173     // Check for hashing null object
4174     obj = null_check_receiver();
4175     if (stopped())  return true;        // unconditionally null
4176     result_reg->init_req(_null_path, top());
4177     result_val->init_req(_null_path, top());
4178   } else {
4179     // Do a null check, and return zero if null.
4180     // System.identityHashCode(null) == 0
4181     Node* null_ctl = top();
4182     obj = null_check_oop(obj, &null_ctl);
4183     result_reg->init_req(_null_path, null_ctl);
4184     result_val->init_req(_null_path, _gvn.intcon(0));
4185   }
4186 
4187   // Unconditionally null?  Then return right away.
4188   if (stopped()) {
4189     set_control( result_reg->in(_null_path));
4190     if (!stopped())
4191       set_result(result_val->in(_null_path));
4192     return true;
4193   }
4194 
4195   // We only go to the fast case code if we pass a number of guards.  The
4196   // paths which do not pass are accumulated in the slow_region.
4197   RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
4198   record_for_igvn(slow_region);
4199 
4200   // If this is a virtual call, we generate a funny guard.  We pull out
4201   // the vtable entry corresponding to hashCode() from the target object.
4202   // If the target method which we are calling happens to be the native
4203   // Object hashCode() method, we pass the guard.  We do not need this
4204   // guard for non-virtual calls -- the caller is known to be the native
4205   // Object hashCode().
4206   if (is_virtual) {
4207     // After null check, get the object's klass.
4208     Node* obj_klass = load_object_klass(obj);
4209     generate_virtual_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4210   }
4211 
4212   // Get the header out of the object, use LoadMarkNode when available
4213   Node* header_addr = basic_plus_adr(obj, oopDesc::mark_offset_in_bytes());
4214   // The control of the load must be NULL. Otherwise, the load can move before
4215   // the null check after castPP removal.
4216   Node* no_ctrl = NULL;
4217   Node* header = make_load(no_ctrl, header_addr, TypeX_X, TypeX_X->basic_type(), MemNode::unordered);
4218 
4219   // Test the header to see if it is unlocked.
4220   // This also serves as guard against inline types (they have the always_locked_pattern set).
4221   Node *lock_mask      = _gvn.MakeConX(markWord::biased_lock_mask_in_place);
4222   Node *lmasked_header = _gvn.transform(new AndXNode(header, lock_mask));
4223   Node *unlocked_val   = _gvn.MakeConX(markWord::unlocked_value);
4224   Node *chk_unlocked   = _gvn.transform(new CmpXNode( lmasked_header, unlocked_val));
4225   Node *test_unlocked  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode( chk_unlocked, BoolTest::ne));
4226 
4227   generate_slow_guard(test_unlocked, slow_region);
4228 
4229   // Get the hash value and check to see that it has been properly assigned.
4230   // We depend on hash_mask being at most 32 bits and avoid the use of
4231   // hash_mask_in_place because it could be larger than 32 bits in a 64-bit
4232   // vm: see markWord.hpp.
4233   Node *hash_mask      = _gvn.intcon(markWord::hash_mask);
4234   Node *hash_shift     = _gvn.intcon(markWord::hash_shift);
4235   Node *hshifted_header= _gvn.transform(new URShiftXNode(header, hash_shift));
4236   // This hack lets the hash bits live anywhere in the mark object now, as long
4237   // as the shift drops the relevant bits into the low 32 bits.  Note that
4238   // Java spec says that HashCode is an int so there's no point in capturing
4239   // an 'X'-sized hashcode (32 in 32-bit build or 64 in 64-bit build).
4240   hshifted_header      = ConvX2I(hshifted_header);
4241   Node *hash_val       = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(hshifted_header, hash_mask));
4242 
4243   Node *no_hash_val    = _gvn.intcon(markWord::no_hash);
4244   Node *chk_assigned   = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode( hash_val, no_hash_val));
4245   Node *test_assigned  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode( chk_assigned, BoolTest::eq));
4246 
4247   generate_slow_guard(test_assigned, slow_region);
4248 
4249   Node* init_mem = reset_memory();
4250   // fill in the rest of the null path:
4251   result_io ->init_req(_null_path, i_o());
4252   result_mem->init_req(_null_path, init_mem);
4253 
4254   result_val->init_req(_fast_path, hash_val);
4255   result_reg->init_req(_fast_path, control());
4256   result_io ->init_req(_fast_path, i_o());
4257   result_mem->init_req(_fast_path, init_mem);
4258 
4259   // Generate code for the slow case.  We make a call to hashCode().
4260   set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
4261   if (!stopped()) {
4262     // No need for PreserveJVMState, because we're using up the present state.
4263     set_all_memory(init_mem);
4264     vmIntrinsics::ID hashCode_id = is_static ? vmIntrinsics::_identityHashCode : vmIntrinsics::_hashCode;
4265     CallJavaNode* slow_call = generate_method_call(hashCode_id, is_virtual, is_static);
4266     Node* slow_result = set_results_for_java_call(slow_call);
4267     // this->control() comes from set_results_for_java_call
4268     result_reg->init_req(_slow_path, control());
4269     result_val->init_req(_slow_path, slow_result);
4270     result_io  ->set_req(_slow_path, i_o());
4271     result_mem ->set_req(_slow_path, reset_memory());
4272   }
4273 
4274   // Return the combined state.
4275   set_i_o(        _gvn.transform(result_io)  );
4276   set_all_memory( _gvn.transform(result_mem));
4277 
4278   set_result(result_reg, result_val);
4279   return true;
4280 }
4281 
4282 //---------------------------inline_native_getClass----------------------------
4283 // public final native Class<?> java.lang.Object.getClass();
4284 //
4285 // Build special case code for calls to getClass on an object.
4286 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_getClass() {
4287   Node* obj = argument(0);
4288   if (obj->is_InlineType()) {
4289     ciKlass* vk = _gvn.type(obj)->inline_klass();
4290     set_result(makecon(TypeInstPtr::make(vk->java_mirror())));
4291     return true;
4292   }
4293   obj = null_check_receiver();
4294   if (stopped())  return true;
4295   set_result(load_mirror_from_klass(load_object_klass(obj)));
4296   return true;
4297 }
4298 
4299 //-----------------inline_native_Reflection_getCallerClass---------------------
4300 // public static native Class<?> sun.reflect.Reflection.getCallerClass();
4301 //
4302 // In the presence of deep enough inlining, getCallerClass() becomes a no-op.
4303 //
4304 // NOTE: This code must perform the same logic as JVM_GetCallerClass
4305 // in that it must skip particular security frames and checks for
4306 // caller sensitive methods.
4307 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_Reflection_getCallerClass() {
4308 #ifndef PRODUCT
4309   if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4310     tty->print_cr("Attempting to inline sun.reflect.Reflection.getCallerClass");
4311   }
4312 #endif
4313 
4314   if (!jvms()->has_method()) {
4315 #ifndef PRODUCT
4316     if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4317       tty->print_cr("  Bailing out because intrinsic was inlined at top level");
4318     }
4319 #endif
4320     return false;
4321   }
4322 
4323   // Walk back up the JVM state to find the caller at the required
4324   // depth.
4325   JVMState* caller_jvms = jvms();
4326 
4327   // Cf. JVM_GetCallerClass
4328   // NOTE: Start the loop at depth 1 because the current JVM state does
4329   // not include the Reflection.getCallerClass() frame.
4330   for (int n = 1; caller_jvms != NULL; caller_jvms = caller_jvms->caller(), n++) {
4331     ciMethod* m = caller_jvms->method();
4332     switch (n) {
4333     case 0:
4334       fatal("current JVM state does not include the Reflection.getCallerClass frame");
4335       break;
4336     case 1:
4337       // Frame 0 and 1 must be caller sensitive (see JVM_GetCallerClass).
4338       if (!m->caller_sensitive()) {
4339 #ifndef PRODUCT
4340         if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4341           tty->print_cr("  Bailing out: CallerSensitive annotation expected at frame %d", n);
4342         }
4343 #endif
4344         return false;  // bail-out; let JVM_GetCallerClass do the work
4345       }
4346       break;
4347     default:
4348       if (!m->is_ignored_by_security_stack_walk()) {
4349         // We have reached the desired frame; return the holder class.
4350         // Acquire method holder as java.lang.Class and push as constant.
4351         ciInstanceKlass* caller_klass = caller_jvms->method()->holder();
4352         ciInstance* caller_mirror = caller_klass->java_mirror();
4353         set_result(makecon(TypeInstPtr::make(caller_mirror)));
4354 
4355 #ifndef PRODUCT
4356         if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4357           tty->print_cr("  Succeeded: caller = %d) %s.%s, JVMS depth = %d", n, caller_klass->name()->as_utf8(), caller_jvms->method()->name()->as_utf8(), jvms()->depth());
4358           tty->print_cr("  JVM state at this point:");
4359           for (int i = jvms()->depth(), n = 1; i >= 1; i--, n++) {
4360             ciMethod* m = jvms()->of_depth(i)->method();
4361             tty->print_cr("   %d) %s.%s", n, m->holder()->name()->as_utf8(), m->name()->as_utf8());
4362           }
4363         }
4364 #endif
4365         return true;
4366       }
4367       break;
4368     }
4369   }
4370 
4371 #ifndef PRODUCT
4372   if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4373     tty->print_cr("  Bailing out because caller depth exceeded inlining depth = %d", jvms()->depth());
4374     tty->print_cr("  JVM state at this point:");
4375     for (int i = jvms()->depth(), n = 1; i >= 1; i--, n++) {
4376       ciMethod* m = jvms()->of_depth(i)->method();
4377       tty->print_cr("   %d) %s.%s", n, m->holder()->name()->as_utf8(), m->name()->as_utf8());
4378     }
4379   }
4380 #endif
4381 
4382   return false;  // bail-out; let JVM_GetCallerClass do the work
4383 }
4384 
4385 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fp_conversions(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
4386   Node* arg = argument(0);
4387   Node* result = NULL;
4388 
4389   switch (id) {
4390   case vmIntrinsics::_floatToRawIntBits:    result = new MoveF2INode(arg);  break;
4391   case vmIntrinsics::_intBitsToFloat:       result = new MoveI2FNode(arg);  break;
4392   case vmIntrinsics::_doubleToRawLongBits:  result = new MoveD2LNode(arg);  break;
4393   case vmIntrinsics::_longBitsToDouble:     result = new MoveL2DNode(arg);  break;
4394 
4395   case vmIntrinsics::_doubleToLongBits: {
4396     // two paths (plus control) merge in a wood
4397     RegionNode *r = new RegionNode(3);
4398     Node *phi = new PhiNode(r, TypeLong::LONG);
4399 
4400     Node *cmpisnan = _gvn.transform(new CmpDNode(arg, arg));
4401     // Build the boolean node
4402     Node *bolisnan = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmpisnan, BoolTest::ne));
4403 
4404     // Branch either way.
4405     // NaN case is less traveled, which makes all the difference.
4406     IfNode *ifisnan = create_and_xform_if(control(), bolisnan, PROB_STATIC_FREQUENT, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
4407     Node *opt_isnan = _gvn.transform(ifisnan);
4408     assert( opt_isnan->is_If(), "Expect an IfNode");
4409     IfNode *opt_ifisnan = (IfNode*)opt_isnan;
4410     Node *iftrue = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(opt_ifisnan));
4411 
4412     set_control(iftrue);
4413 
4414     static const jlong nan_bits = CONST64(0x7ff8000000000000);
4415     Node *slow_result = longcon(nan_bits); // return NaN
4416     phi->init_req(1, _gvn.transform( slow_result ));
4417     r->init_req(1, iftrue);
4418 
4419     // Else fall through
4420     Node *iffalse = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(opt_ifisnan));
4421     set_control(iffalse);
4422 
4423     phi->init_req(2, _gvn.transform(new MoveD2LNode(arg)));
4424     r->init_req(2, iffalse);
4425 
4426     // Post merge
4427     set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
4428     record_for_igvn(r);
4429 
4430     C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4431     result = phi;
4432     assert(result->bottom_type()->isa_long(), "must be");
4433     break;
4434   }
4435 
4436   case vmIntrinsics::_floatToIntBits: {
4437     // two paths (plus control) merge in a wood
4438     RegionNode *r = new RegionNode(3);
4439     Node *phi = new PhiNode(r, TypeInt::INT);
4440 
4441     Node *cmpisnan = _gvn.transform(new CmpFNode(arg, arg));
4442     // Build the boolean node
4443     Node *bolisnan = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmpisnan, BoolTest::ne));
4444 
4445     // Branch either way.
4446     // NaN case is less traveled, which makes all the difference.
4447     IfNode *ifisnan = create_and_xform_if(control(), bolisnan, PROB_STATIC_FREQUENT, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
4448     Node *opt_isnan = _gvn.transform(ifisnan);
4449     assert( opt_isnan->is_If(), "Expect an IfNode");
4450     IfNode *opt_ifisnan = (IfNode*)opt_isnan;
4451     Node *iftrue = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(opt_ifisnan));
4452 
4453     set_control(iftrue);
4454 
4455     static const jint nan_bits = 0x7fc00000;
4456     Node *slow_result = makecon(TypeInt::make(nan_bits)); // return NaN
4457     phi->init_req(1, _gvn.transform( slow_result ));
4458     r->init_req(1, iftrue);
4459 
4460     // Else fall through
4461     Node *iffalse = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(opt_ifisnan));
4462     set_control(iffalse);
4463 
4464     phi->init_req(2, _gvn.transform(new MoveF2INode(arg)));
4465     r->init_req(2, iffalse);
4466 
4467     // Post merge
4468     set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
4469     record_for_igvn(r);
4470 
4471     C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4472     result = phi;
4473     assert(result->bottom_type()->isa_int(), "must be");
4474     break;
4475   }
4476 
4477   default:
4478     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
4479     break;
4480   }
4481   set_result(_gvn.transform(result));
4482   return true;
4483 }
4484 
4485 //----------------------inline_unsafe_copyMemory-------------------------
4486 // public native void Unsafe.copyMemory0(Object srcBase, long srcOffset, Object destBase, long destOffset, long bytes);
4487 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_unsafe_copyMemory() {
4488   if (callee()->is_static())  return false;  // caller must have the capability!
4489   null_check_receiver();  // null-check receiver
4490   if (stopped())  return true;
4491 
4492   C->set_has_unsafe_access(true);  // Mark eventual nmethod as "unsafe".
4493 
4494   Node* src_ptr =         argument(1);   // type: oop
4495   Node* src_off = ConvL2X(argument(2));  // type: long
4496   Node* dst_ptr =         argument(4);   // type: oop
4497   Node* dst_off = ConvL2X(argument(5));  // type: long
4498   Node* size    = ConvL2X(argument(7));  // type: long
4499 
4500   assert(Unsafe_field_offset_to_byte_offset(11) == 11,
4501          "fieldOffset must be byte-scaled");
4502 
4503   Node* src = make_unsafe_address(src_ptr, src_off, ACCESS_READ);
4504   Node* dst = make_unsafe_address(dst_ptr, dst_off, ACCESS_WRITE);
4505 
4506   // Conservatively insert a memory barrier on all memory slices.
4507   // Do not let writes of the copy source or destination float below the copy.
4508   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4509 
4510   Node* thread = _gvn.transform(new ThreadLocalNode());
4511   Node* doing_unsafe_access_addr = basic_plus_adr(top(), thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::doing_unsafe_access_offset()));
4512   BasicType doing_unsafe_access_bt = T_BYTE;
4513   assert((sizeof(bool) * CHAR_BIT) == 8, "not implemented");
4514 
4515   // update volatile field
4516   store_to_memory(control(), doing_unsafe_access_addr, intcon(1), doing_unsafe_access_bt, Compile::AliasIdxRaw, MemNode::unordered);
4517 
4518   // Call it.  Note that the length argument is not scaled.
4519   make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
4520                     OptoRuntime::fast_arraycopy_Type(),
4521                     StubRoutines::unsafe_arraycopy(),
4522                     "unsafe_arraycopy",
4523                     TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM,
4524                     src, dst, size XTOP);
4525 
4526   store_to_memory(control(), doing_unsafe_access_addr, intcon(0), doing_unsafe_access_bt, Compile::AliasIdxRaw, MemNode::unordered);
4527 
4528   // Do not let reads of the copy destination float above the copy.
4529   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4530 
4531   return true;
4532 }
4533 
4534 //------------------------clone_coping-----------------------------------
4535 // Helper function for inline_native_clone.
4536 void LibraryCallKit::copy_to_clone(Node* obj, Node* alloc_obj, Node* obj_size, bool is_array) {
4537   assert(obj_size != NULL, "");
4538   Node* raw_obj = alloc_obj->in(1);
4539   assert(alloc_obj->is_CheckCastPP() && raw_obj->is_Proj() && raw_obj->in(0)->is_Allocate(), "");
4540 
4541   AllocateNode* alloc = NULL;
4542   if (ReduceBulkZeroing) {
4543     // We will be completely responsible for initializing this object -
4544     // mark Initialize node as complete.
4545     alloc = AllocateNode::Ideal_allocation(alloc_obj, &_gvn);
4546     // The object was just allocated - there should be no any stores!
4547     guarantee(alloc != NULL && alloc->maybe_set_complete(&_gvn), "");
4548     // Mark as complete_with_arraycopy so that on AllocateNode
4549     // expansion, we know this AllocateNode is initialized by an array
4550     // copy and a StoreStore barrier exists after the array copy.
4551     alloc->initialization()->set_complete_with_arraycopy();
4552   }
4553 
4554   Node* size = _gvn.transform(obj_size);
4555   // Exclude the header but include array length to copy by 8 bytes words.
4556   // Can't use base_offset_in_bytes(bt) since basic type is unknown.
4557   int base_off = BarrierSetC2::arraycopy_payload_base_offset(is_array);
4558   Node* countx = size;
4559   countx = _gvn.transform(new SubXNode(countx, MakeConX(base_off)));
4560   countx = _gvn.transform(new URShiftXNode(countx, intcon(LogBytesPerLong)));
4561 
4562   access_clone(obj, alloc_obj, countx, is_array);
4563 
4564   // Do not let reads from the cloned object float above the arraycopy.
4565   if (alloc != NULL) {
4566     // Do not let stores that initialize this object be reordered with
4567     // a subsequent store that would make this object accessible by
4568     // other threads.
4569     // Record what AllocateNode this StoreStore protects so that
4570     // escape analysis can go from the MemBarStoreStoreNode to the
4571     // AllocateNode and eliminate the MemBarStoreStoreNode if possible
4572     // based on the escape status of the AllocateNode.
4573     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarStoreStore, alloc->proj_out_or_null(AllocateNode::RawAddress));
4574   } else {
4575     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4576   }
4577 }
4578 
4579 //------------------------inline_native_clone----------------------------
4580 // protected native Object java.lang.Object.clone();
4581 //
4582 // Here are the simple edge cases:
4583 //  null receiver => normal trap
4584 //  virtual and clone was overridden => slow path to out-of-line clone
4585 //  not cloneable or finalizer => slow path to out-of-line Object.clone
4586 //
4587 // The general case has two steps, allocation and copying.
4588 // Allocation has two cases, and uses GraphKit::new_instance or new_array.
4589 //
4590 // Copying also has two cases, oop arrays and everything else.
4591 // Oop arrays use arrayof_oop_arraycopy (same as System.arraycopy).
4592 // Everything else uses the tight inline loop supplied by CopyArrayNode.
4593 //
4594 // These steps fold up nicely if and when the cloned object's klass
4595 // can be sharply typed as an object array, a type array, or an instance.
4596 //
4597 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_clone(bool is_virtual) {
4598   PhiNode* result_val;
4599 
4600   // Set the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
4601   // the bytecode that invokes Object.clone if deoptimization happens.
4602   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
4603     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
4604 
4605     Node* obj = argument(0);
4606     if (obj->is_InlineType()) {
4607       return false;
4608     }
4609 
4610     obj = null_check_receiver();
4611     if (stopped())  return true;
4612 
4613     const TypeOopPtr* obj_type = _gvn.type(obj)->is_oopptr();
4614 
4615     // If we are going to clone an instance, we need its exact type to
4616     // know the number and types of fields to convert the clone to
4617     // loads/stores. Maybe a speculative type can help us.
4618     if (!obj_type->klass_is_exact() &&
4619         obj_type->speculative_type() != NULL &&
4620         obj_type->speculative_type()->is_instance_klass() &&
4621         !obj_type->speculative_type()->is_inlinetype()) {
4622       ciInstanceKlass* spec_ik = obj_type->speculative_type()->as_instance_klass();
4623       if (spec_ik->nof_nonstatic_fields() <= ArrayCopyLoadStoreMaxElem &&
4624           !spec_ik->has_injected_fields()) {
4625         ciKlass* k = obj_type->klass();
4626         if (!k->is_instance_klass() ||
4627             k->as_instance_klass()->is_interface() ||
4628             k->as_instance_klass()->has_subklass()) {
4629           obj = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(obj, obj_type->speculative_type(), false);
4630         }
4631       }
4632     }
4633 
4634     // Conservatively insert a memory barrier on all memory slices.
4635     // Do not let writes into the original float below the clone.
4636     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4637 
4638     // paths into result_reg:
4639     enum {
4640       _slow_path = 1,     // out-of-line call to clone method (virtual or not)
4641       _objArray_path,     // plain array allocation, plus arrayof_oop_arraycopy
4642       _array_path,        // plain array allocation, plus arrayof_long_arraycopy
4643       _instance_path,     // plain instance allocation, plus arrayof_long_arraycopy
4644       PATH_LIMIT
4645     };
4646     RegionNode* result_reg = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
4647     result_val             = new PhiNode(result_reg, TypeInstPtr::NOTNULL);
4648     PhiNode*    result_i_o = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::ABIO);
4649     PhiNode*    result_mem = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::MEMORY, TypePtr::BOTTOM);
4650     record_for_igvn(result_reg);
4651 
4652     Node* obj_klass = load_object_klass(obj);
4653     // We only go to the fast case code if we pass a number of guards.
4654     // The paths which do not pass are accumulated in the slow_region.
4655     RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
4656     record_for_igvn(slow_region);
4657 
4658     Node* array_ctl = generate_array_guard(obj_klass, (RegionNode*)NULL);
4659     if (array_ctl != NULL) {
4660       // It's an array.
4661       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4662       set_control(array_ctl);
4663 
4664       BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
4665       if (bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(true, T_OBJECT, true, BarrierSetC2::Parsing) &&
4666           (!obj_type->isa_aryptr() || !obj_type->is_aryptr()->is_not_flat())) {
4667         // Flattened inline type array may have object field that would require a
4668         // write barrier. Conservatively, go to slow path.
4669         generate_flatArray_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4670       }
4671 
4672       if (!stopped()) {
4673         Node* obj_length = load_array_length(obj);
4674         Node* obj_size  = NULL;
4675         Node* alloc_obj = new_array(obj_klass, obj_length, 0, &obj_size, /*deoptimize_on_exception=*/true);
4676 
4677         BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
4678         if (bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(true, T_OBJECT, true, BarrierSetC2::Parsing)) {
4679           // If it is an oop array, it requires very special treatment,
4680           // because gc barriers are required when accessing the array.
4681           Node* is_obja = generate_objArray_guard(obj_klass, (RegionNode*)NULL);
4682           if (is_obja != NULL) {
4683             PreserveJVMState pjvms2(this);
4684             set_control(is_obja);
4685             // Generate a direct call to the right arraycopy function(s).
4686             Node* alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(alloc_obj, NULL);
4687             ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, obj, intcon(0), alloc_obj, intcon(0), obj_length, alloc != NULL, false);
4688             ac->set_clone_oop_array();
4689             Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
4690             assert(n == ac, "cannot disappear");
4691             ac->connect_outputs(this, /*deoptimize_on_exception=*/true);
4692 
4693             result_reg->init_req(_objArray_path, control());
4694             result_val->init_req(_objArray_path, alloc_obj);
4695             result_i_o ->set_req(_objArray_path, i_o());
4696             result_mem ->set_req(_objArray_path, reset_memory());
4697           }
4698         }
4699         // Otherwise, there are no barriers to worry about.
4700         // (We can dispense with card marks if we know the allocation
4701         //  comes out of eden (TLAB)...  In fact, ReduceInitialCardMarks
4702         //  causes the non-eden paths to take compensating steps to
4703         //  simulate a fresh allocation, so that no further
4704         //  card marks are required in compiled code to initialize
4705         //  the object.)
4706 
4707         if (!stopped()) {
4708           copy_to_clone(obj, alloc_obj, obj_size, true);
4709 
4710           // Present the results of the copy.
4711           result_reg->init_req(_array_path, control());
4712           result_val->init_req(_array_path, alloc_obj);
4713           result_i_o ->set_req(_array_path, i_o());
4714           result_mem ->set_req(_array_path, reset_memory());
4715         }
4716       }
4717     }
4718 
4719     if (!stopped()) {
4720       // It's an instance (we did array above).  Make the slow-path tests.
4721       // If this is a virtual call, we generate a funny guard.  We grab
4722       // the vtable entry corresponding to clone() from the target object.
4723       // If the target method which we are calling happens to be the
4724       // Object clone() method, we pass the guard.  We do not need this
4725       // guard for non-virtual calls; the caller is known to be the native
4726       // Object clone().
4727       if (is_virtual) {
4728         generate_virtual_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4729       }
4730 
4731       // The object must be easily cloneable and must not have a finalizer.
4732       // Both of these conditions may be checked in a single test.
4733       // We could optimize the test further, but we don't care.
4734       generate_access_flags_guard(obj_klass,
4735                                   // Test both conditions:
4736                                   JVM_ACC_IS_CLONEABLE_FAST | JVM_ACC_HAS_FINALIZER,
4737                                   // Must be cloneable but not finalizer:
4738                                   JVM_ACC_IS_CLONEABLE_FAST,
4739                                   slow_region);
4740     }
4741 
4742     if (!stopped()) {
4743       // It's an instance, and it passed the slow-path tests.
4744       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4745       Node* obj_size  = NULL;
4746       // Need to deoptimize on exception from allocation since Object.clone intrinsic
4747       // is reexecuted if deoptimization occurs and there could be problems when merging
4748       // exception state between multiple Object.clone versions (reexecute=true vs reexecute=false).
4749       Node* alloc_obj = new_instance(obj_klass, NULL, &obj_size, /*deoptimize_on_exception=*/true);
4750 
4751       copy_to_clone(obj, alloc_obj, obj_size, false);
4752 
4753       // Present the results of the slow call.
4754       result_reg->init_req(_instance_path, control());
4755       result_val->init_req(_instance_path, alloc_obj);
4756       result_i_o ->set_req(_instance_path, i_o());
4757       result_mem ->set_req(_instance_path, reset_memory());
4758     }
4759 
4760     // Generate code for the slow case.  We make a call to clone().
4761     set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
4762     if (!stopped()) {
4763       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4764       CallJavaNode* slow_call = generate_method_call(vmIntrinsics::_clone, is_virtual);
4765       // We need to deoptimize on exception (see comment above)
4766       Node* slow_result = set_results_for_java_call(slow_call, false, /* deoptimize */ true);
4767       // this->control() comes from set_results_for_java_call
4768       result_reg->init_req(_slow_path, control());
4769       result_val->init_req(_slow_path, slow_result);
4770       result_i_o ->set_req(_slow_path, i_o());
4771       result_mem ->set_req(_slow_path, reset_memory());
4772     }
4773 
4774     // Return the combined state.
4775     set_control(    _gvn.transform(result_reg));
4776     set_i_o(        _gvn.transform(result_i_o));
4777     set_all_memory( _gvn.transform(result_mem));
4778   } // original reexecute is set back here
4779 
4780   set_result(_gvn.transform(result_val));
4781   return true;
4782 }
4783 
4784 // If we have a tightly coupled allocation, the arraycopy may take care
4785 // of the array initialization. If one of the guards we insert between
4786 // the allocation and the arraycopy causes a deoptimization, an
4787 // unitialized array will escape the compiled method. To prevent that
4788 // we set the JVM state for uncommon traps between the allocation and
4789 // the arraycopy to the state before the allocation so, in case of
4790 // deoptimization, we'll reexecute the allocation and the
4791 // initialization.
4792 JVMState* LibraryCallKit::arraycopy_restore_alloc_state(AllocateArrayNode* alloc, int& saved_reexecute_sp) {
4793   if (alloc != NULL) {
4794     ciMethod* trap_method = alloc->jvms()->method();
4795     int trap_bci = alloc->jvms()->bci();
4796 
4797     if (!C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic) &&
4798         !C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_null_check)) {
4799       // Make sure there's no store between the allocation and the
4800       // arraycopy otherwise visible side effects could be rexecuted
4801       // in case of deoptimization and cause incorrect execution.
4802       bool no_interfering_store = true;
4803       Node* mem = alloc->in(TypeFunc::Memory);
4804       if (mem->is_MergeMem()) {
4805         for (MergeMemStream mms(merged_memory(), mem->as_MergeMem()); mms.next_non_empty2(); ) {
4806           Node* n = mms.memory();
4807           if (n != mms.memory2() && !(n->is_Proj() && n->in(0) == alloc->initialization())) {
4808             assert(n->is_Store(), "what else?");
4809             no_interfering_store = false;
4810             break;
4811           }
4812         }
4813       } else {
4814         for (MergeMemStream mms(merged_memory()); mms.next_non_empty(); ) {
4815           Node* n = mms.memory();
4816           if (n != mem && !(n->is_Proj() && n->in(0) == alloc->initialization())) {
4817             assert(n->is_Store(), "what else?");
4818             no_interfering_store = false;
4819             break;
4820           }
4821         }
4822       }
4823 
4824       if (no_interfering_store) {
4825         JVMState* old_jvms = alloc->jvms()->clone_shallow(C);
4826         uint size = alloc->req();
4827         SafePointNode* sfpt = new SafePointNode(size, old_jvms);
4828         old_jvms->set_map(sfpt);
4829         for (uint i = 0; i < size; i++) {
4830           sfpt->init_req(i, alloc->in(i));
4831         }
4832         // re-push array length for deoptimization
4833         sfpt->ins_req(old_jvms->stkoff() + old_jvms->sp(), alloc->in(AllocateNode::ALength));
4834         old_jvms->set_sp(old_jvms->sp()+1);
4835         old_jvms->set_monoff(old_jvms->monoff()+1);
4836         old_jvms->set_scloff(old_jvms->scloff()+1);
4837         old_jvms->set_endoff(old_jvms->endoff()+1);
4838         old_jvms->set_should_reexecute(true);
4839 
4840         sfpt->set_i_o(map()->i_o());
4841         sfpt->set_memory(map()->memory());
4842         sfpt->set_control(map()->control());
4843 
4844         JVMState* saved_jvms = jvms();
4845         saved_reexecute_sp = _reexecute_sp;
4846 
4847         set_jvms(sfpt->jvms());
4848         _reexecute_sp = jvms()->sp();
4849 
4850         return saved_jvms;
4851       }
4852     }
4853   }
4854   return NULL;
4855 }
4856 
4857 // In case of a deoptimization, we restart execution at the
4858 // allocation, allocating a new array. We would leave an uninitialized
4859 // array in the heap that GCs wouldn't expect. Move the allocation
4860 // after the traps so we don't allocate the array if we
4861 // deoptimize. This is possible because tightly_coupled_allocation()
4862 // guarantees there's no observer of the allocated array at this point
4863 // and the control flow is simple enough.
4864 void LibraryCallKit::arraycopy_move_allocation_here(AllocateArrayNode* alloc, Node* dest, JVMState* saved_jvms,
4865                                                     int saved_reexecute_sp, uint new_idx) {
4866   if (saved_jvms != NULL && !stopped()) {
4867     assert(alloc != NULL, "only with a tightly coupled allocation");
4868     // restore JVM state to the state at the arraycopy
4869     saved_jvms->map()->set_control(map()->control());
4870     assert(saved_jvms->map()->memory() == map()->memory(), "memory state changed?");
4871     assert(saved_jvms->map()->i_o() == map()->i_o(), "IO state changed?");
4872     // If we've improved the types of some nodes (null check) while
4873     // emitting the guards, propagate them to the current state
4874     map()->replaced_nodes().apply(saved_jvms->map(), new_idx);
4875     set_jvms(saved_jvms);
4876     _reexecute_sp = saved_reexecute_sp;
4877 
4878     // Remove the allocation from above the guards
4879     CallProjections* callprojs = alloc->extract_projections(true);
4880     InitializeNode* init = alloc->initialization();
4881     Node* alloc_mem = alloc->in(TypeFunc::Memory);
4882     C->gvn_replace_by(callprojs->fallthrough_ioproj, alloc->in(TypeFunc::I_O));
4883     C->gvn_replace_by(init->proj_out(TypeFunc::Memory), alloc_mem);
4884     C->gvn_replace_by(init->proj_out(TypeFunc::Control), alloc->in(0));
4885 
4886     // move the allocation here (after the guards)
4887     _gvn.hash_delete(alloc);
4888     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::Control, control());
4889     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::I_O, i_o());
4890     Node *mem = reset_memory();
4891     set_all_memory(mem);
4892     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::Memory, mem);
4893     set_control(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Control));
4894     set_i_o(callprojs->fallthrough_ioproj);
4895 
4896     // Update memory as done in GraphKit::set_output_for_allocation()
4897     const TypeInt* length_type = _gvn.find_int_type(alloc->in(AllocateNode::ALength));
4898     const TypeOopPtr* ary_type = _gvn.type(alloc->in(AllocateNode::KlassNode))->is_klassptr()->as_instance_type();
4899     if (ary_type->isa_aryptr() && length_type != NULL) {
4900       ary_type = ary_type->is_aryptr()->cast_to_size(length_type);
4901     }
4902     const TypePtr* telemref = ary_type->add_offset(Type::OffsetBot);
4903     int            elemidx  = C->get_alias_index(telemref);
4904     set_memory(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Memory), Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
4905     set_memory(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Memory), elemidx);
4906 
4907     Node* allocx = _gvn.transform(alloc);
4908     assert(allocx == alloc, "where has the allocation gone?");
4909     assert(dest->is_CheckCastPP(), "not an allocation result?");
4910 
4911     _gvn.hash_delete(dest);
4912     dest->set_req(0, control());
4913     Node* destx = _gvn.transform(dest);
4914     assert(destx == dest, "where has the allocation result gone?");
4915   }
4916 }
4917 
4918 
4919 //------------------------------inline_arraycopy-----------------------
4920 // public static native void java.lang.System.arraycopy(Object src,  int  srcPos,
4921 //                                                      Object dest, int destPos,
4922 //                                                      int length);
4923 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_arraycopy() {
4924   // Get the arguments.
4925   Node* src         = argument(0);  // type: oop
4926   Node* src_offset  = argument(1);  // type: int
4927   Node* dest        = argument(2);  // type: oop
4928   Node* dest_offset = argument(3);  // type: int
4929   Node* length      = argument(4);  // type: int
4930 
4931   uint new_idx = C->unique();
4932 
4933   // Check for allocation before we add nodes that would confuse
4934   // tightly_coupled_allocation()
4935   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4936 
4937   int saved_reexecute_sp = -1;
4938   JVMState* saved_jvms = arraycopy_restore_alloc_state(alloc, saved_reexecute_sp);
4939   // See arraycopy_restore_alloc_state() comment
4940   // if alloc == NULL we don't have to worry about a tightly coupled allocation so we can emit all needed guards
4941   // if saved_jvms != NULL (then alloc != NULL) then we can handle guards and a tightly coupled allocation
4942   // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we can't emit any guards
4943   bool can_emit_guards = (alloc == NULL || saved_jvms != NULL);
4944 
4945   // The following tests must be performed
4946   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
4947   // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
4948   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4949   // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
4950   // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
4951   // (6) length must not be negative.
4952   // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
4953   // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
4954   // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
4955 
4956   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4957   // always do this here because we need the JVM state for uncommon traps
4958   Node* null_ctl = top();
4959   src  = saved_jvms != NULL ? null_check_oop(src, &null_ctl, true, true) : null_check(src,  T_ARRAY);
4960   assert(null_ctl->is_top(), "no null control here");
4961   dest = null_check(dest, T_ARRAY);
4962 
4963   if (!can_emit_guards) {
4964     // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we don't emit any
4965     // guards but the arraycopy node could still take advantage of a
4966     // tightly allocated allocation. tightly_coupled_allocation() is
4967     // called again to make sure it takes the null check above into
4968     // account: the null check is mandatory and if it caused an
4969     // uncommon trap to be emitted then the allocation can't be
4970     // considered tightly coupled in this context.
4971     alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4972   }
4973 
4974   bool validated = false;
4975 
4976   const Type* src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
4977   const Type* dest_type = _gvn.type(dest);
4978   const TypeAryPtr* top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
4979   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
4980 
4981   // Do we have the type of src?
4982   bool has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
4983   // Do we have the type of dest?
4984   bool has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
4985   // Is the type for src from speculation?
4986   bool src_spec = false;
4987   // Is the type for dest from speculation?
4988   bool dest_spec = false;
4989 
4990   if ((!has_src || !has_dest) && can_emit_guards) {
4991     // We don't have sufficient type information, let's see if
4992     // speculative types can help. We need to have types for both src
4993     // and dest so that it pays off.
4994 
4995     // Do we already have or could we have type information for src
4996     bool could_have_src = has_src;
4997     // Do we already have or could we have type information for dest
4998     bool could_have_dest = has_dest;
4999 
5000     ciKlass* src_k = NULL;
5001     if (!has_src) {
5002       src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5003       if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
5004         could_have_src = true;
5005       }
5006     }
5007 
5008     ciKlass* dest_k = NULL;
5009     if (!has_dest) {
5010       dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5011       if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
5012         could_have_dest = true;
5013       }
5014     }
5015 
5016     if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
5017       // This is going to pay off so emit the required guards
5018       if (!has_src) {
5019         src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
5020         src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
5021         top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5022         has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
5023         src_spec = true;
5024       }
5025       if (!has_dest) {
5026         dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
5027         dest_type  = _gvn.type(dest);
5028         top_dest  = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
5029         has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
5030         dest_spec = true;
5031       }
5032     }
5033   }
5034 
5035   if (has_src && has_dest && can_emit_guards) {
5036     BasicType src_elem  = top_src->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5037     BasicType dest_elem = top_dest->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5038     if (is_reference_type(src_elem))   src_elem  = T_OBJECT;
5039     if (is_reference_type(dest_elem))  dest_elem = T_OBJECT;
5040 
5041     if (src_elem == dest_elem && src_elem == T_OBJECT) {
5042       // If both arrays are object arrays then having the exact types
5043       // for both will remove the need for a subtype check at runtime
5044       // before the call and may make it possible to pick a faster copy
5045       // routine (without a subtype check on every element)
5046       // Do we have the exact type of src?
5047       bool could_have_src = src_spec;
5048       // Do we have the exact type of dest?
5049       bool could_have_dest = dest_spec;
5050       ciKlass* src_k = top_src->klass();
5051       ciKlass* dest_k = top_dest->klass();
5052       if (!src_spec) {
5053         src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5054         if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
5055           could_have_src = true;
5056         }
5057       }
5058       if (!dest_spec) {
5059         dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5060         if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
5061           could_have_dest = true;
5062         }
5063       }
5064       if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
5065         // If we can have both exact types, emit the missing guards
5066         if (could_have_src && !src_spec) {
5067           src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
5068         }
5069         if (could_have_dest && !dest_spec) {
5070           dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
5071         }
5072       }
5073     }
5074   }
5075 
5076   ciMethod* trap_method = method();
5077   int trap_bci = bci();
5078   if (saved_jvms != NULL) {
5079     trap_method = alloc->jvms()->method();
5080     trap_bci = alloc->jvms()->bci();
5081   }
5082 
5083   bool negative_length_guard_generated = false;
5084 
5085   if (!C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic) &&
5086       can_emit_guards &&
5087       !src->is_top() && !dest->is_top()) {
5088     // validate arguments: enables transformation the ArrayCopyNode
5089     validated = true;
5090 
5091     RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
5092     record_for_igvn(slow_region);
5093 
5094     // (1) src and dest are arrays.
5095     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(src), slow_region);
5096     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(dest), slow_region);
5097 
5098     // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
5099     // done at macro expansion or at Ideal transformation time
5100 
5101     // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
5102     generate_negative_guard(src_offset, slow_region);
5103 
5104     // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
5105     generate_negative_guard(dest_offset, slow_region);
5106 
5107     // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
5108     generate_limit_guard(src_offset, length,
5109                          load_array_length(src),
5110                          slow_region);
5111 
5112     // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
5113     generate_limit_guard(dest_offset, length,
5114                          load_array_length(dest),
5115                          slow_region);
5116 
5117     // (6) length must not be negative.
5118     // This is also checked in generate_arraycopy() during macro expansion, but
5119     // we also have to check it here for the case where the ArrayCopyNode will
5120     // be eliminated by Escape Analysis.
5121     if (EliminateAllocations) {
5122       generate_negative_guard(length, slow_region);
5123       negative_length_guard_generated = true;
5124     }
5125 
5126     // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
5127     Node* dest_klass = load_object_klass(dest);
5128     if (src != dest) {
5129       Node* not_subtype_ctrl = gen_subtype_check(src, dest_klass);
5130 
5131       if (not_subtype_ctrl != top()) {
5132         PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
5133         set_control(not_subtype_ctrl);
5134         uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
5135                       Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
5136         assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
5137       }
5138     }
5139 
5140     const TypeKlassPtr* dest_klass_t = _gvn.type(dest_klass)->is_klassptr();
5141     const Type* toop = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(dest_klass_t->klass());
5142     src = _gvn.transform(new CheckCastPPNode(control(), src, toop));
5143     src_type = _gvn.type(src);
5144     top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5145 
5146     if (top_dest != NULL && !top_dest->elem()->isa_inlinetype() && !top_dest->is_not_flat()) {
5147       generate_flatArray_guard(dest_klass, slow_region);
5148     }
5149 
5150     if (top_src != NULL && !top_src->elem()->isa_inlinetype() && !top_src->is_not_flat()) {
5151       Node* src_klass = load_object_klass(src);
5152       generate_flatArray_guard(src_klass, slow_region);
5153     }
5154 
5155     {
5156       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
5157       set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
5158       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
5159                     Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
5160       assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
5161     }
5162   }
5163 
5164   arraycopy_move_allocation_here(alloc, dest, saved_jvms, saved_reexecute_sp, new_idx);
5165 
5166   if (stopped()) {
5167     return true;
5168   }
5169 
5170   ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, src, src_offset, dest, dest_offset, length, alloc != NULL, negative_length_guard_generated,
5171                                           // Create LoadRange and LoadKlass nodes for use during macro expansion here
5172                                           // so the compiler has a chance to eliminate them: during macro expansion,
5173                                           // we have to set their control (CastPP nodes are eliminated).
5174                                           load_object_klass(src), load_object_klass(dest),
5175                                           load_array_length(src), load_array_length(dest));
5176 
5177   ac->set_arraycopy(validated);
5178 
5179   Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
5180   if (n == ac) {
5181     ac->connect_outputs(this);
5182   } else {
5183     assert(validated, "shouldn't transform if all arguments not validated");
5184     set_all_memory(n);
5185   }
5186   clear_upper_avx();
5187 
5188 
5189   return true;
5190 }
5191 
5192 
5193 // Helper function which determines if an arraycopy immediately follows
5194 // an allocation, with no intervening tests or other escapes for the object.
5195 AllocateArrayNode*
5196 LibraryCallKit::tightly_coupled_allocation(Node* ptr,
5197                                            RegionNode* slow_region) {
5198   if (stopped())             return NULL;  // no fast path
5199   if (C->AliasLevel() == 0)  return NULL;  // no MergeMems around
5200 
5201   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = AllocateArrayNode::Ideal_array_allocation(ptr, &_gvn);
5202   if (alloc == NULL)  return NULL;
5203 
5204   Node* rawmem = memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
5205   // Is the allocation's memory state untouched?
5206   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0)->is_Initialize())) {
5207     // Bail out if there have been raw-memory effects since the allocation.
5208     // (Example:  There might have been a call or safepoint.)
5209     return NULL;
5210   }
5211   rawmem = rawmem->in(0)->as_Initialize()->memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
5212   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0) == alloc)) {
5213     return NULL;
5214   }
5215 
5216   // There must be no unexpected observers of this allocation.
5217   for (DUIterator_Fast imax, i = ptr->fast_outs(imax); i < imax; i++) {
5218     Node* obs = ptr->fast_out(i);
5219     if (obs != this->map()) {
5220       return NULL;
5221     }
5222   }
5223 
5224   // This arraycopy must unconditionally follow the allocation of the ptr.
5225   Node* alloc_ctl = ptr->in(0);
5226   Node* ctl = control();
5227   while (ctl != alloc_ctl) {
5228     // There may be guards which feed into the slow_region.
5229     // Any other control flow means that we might not get a chance
5230     // to finish initializing the allocated object.
5231     if ((ctl->is_IfFalse() || ctl->is_IfTrue()) && ctl->in(0)->is_If()) {
5232       IfNode* iff = ctl->in(0)->as_If();
5233       Node* not_ctl = iff->proj_out_or_null(1 - ctl->as_Proj()->_con);
5234       assert(not_ctl != NULL && not_ctl != ctl, "found alternate");
5235       if (slow_region != NULL && slow_region->find_edge(not_ctl) >= 1) {
5236         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds the known slow_region.
5237         continue;
5238       }
5239       // One more try:  Various low-level checks bottom out in
5240       // uncommon traps.  If the debug-info of the trap omits
5241       // any reference to the allocation, as we've already
5242       // observed, then there can be no objection to the trap.
5243       bool found_trap = false;
5244       for (DUIterator_Fast jmax, j = not_ctl->fast_outs(jmax); j < jmax; j++) {
5245         Node* obs = not_ctl->fast_out(j);
5246         if (obs->in(0) == not_ctl && obs->is_Call() &&
5247             (obs->as_Call()->entry_point() == SharedRuntime::uncommon_trap_blob()->entry_point())) {
5248           found_trap = true; break;
5249         }
5250       }
5251       if (found_trap) {
5252         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds a harmless uncommon trap.
5253         continue;
5254       }
5255     }
5256     return NULL;
5257   }
5258 
5259   // If we get this far, we have an allocation which immediately
5260   // precedes the arraycopy, and we can take over zeroing the new object.
5261   // The arraycopy will finish the initialization, and provide
5262   // a new control state to which we will anchor the destination pointer.
5263 
5264   return alloc;
5265 }
5266 
5267 //-------------inline_encodeISOArray-----------------------------------
5268 // encode char[] to byte[] in ISO_8859_1
5269 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_encodeISOArray() {
5270   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "encodeISOArray has 5 parameters");
5271   // no receiver since it is static method
5272   Node *src         = argument(0);
5273   Node *src_offset  = argument(1);
5274   Node *dst         = argument(2);
5275   Node *dst_offset  = argument(3);
5276   Node *length      = argument(4);
5277 
5278   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5279   dst = must_be_not_null(dst, true);
5280 
5281   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5282   const Type* dst_type = dst->Value(&_gvn);
5283   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5284   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dst_type->isa_aryptr();
5285   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL ||
5286       top_dest == NULL || top_dest->klass() == NULL) {
5287     // failed array check
5288     return false;
5289   }
5290 
5291   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5292   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5293   BasicType dst_elem = dst_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5294   if (!((src_elem == T_CHAR) || (src_elem== T_BYTE)) || dst_elem != T_BYTE) {
5295     return false;
5296   }
5297 
5298   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, src_offset, T_CHAR);
5299   Node* dst_start = array_element_address(dst, dst_offset, dst_elem);
5300   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5301   // 'dst_start' points to dst array + scaled offset
5302 
5303   const TypeAryPtr* mtype = TypeAryPtr::BYTES;
5304   Node* enc = new EncodeISOArrayNode(control(), memory(mtype), src_start, dst_start, length);
5305   enc = _gvn.transform(enc);
5306   Node* res_mem = _gvn.transform(new SCMemProjNode(enc));
5307   set_memory(res_mem, mtype);
5308   set_result(enc);
5309   clear_upper_avx();
5310 
5311   return true;
5312 }
5313 
5314 //-------------inline_multiplyToLen-----------------------------------
5315 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_multiplyToLen() {
5316   assert(UseMultiplyToLenIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5317 
5318   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::multiplyToLen();
5319   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5320     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5321   }
5322   const char* stubName = "multiplyToLen";
5323 
5324   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "multiplyToLen has 5 parameters");
5325 
5326   // no receiver because it is a static method
5327   Node* x    = argument(0);
5328   Node* xlen = argument(1);
5329   Node* y    = argument(2);
5330   Node* ylen = argument(3);
5331   Node* z    = argument(4);
5332 
5333   x = must_be_not_null(x, true);
5334   y = must_be_not_null(y, true);
5335 
5336   const Type* x_type = x->Value(&_gvn);
5337   const Type* y_type = y->Value(&_gvn);
5338   const TypeAryPtr* top_x = x_type->isa_aryptr();
5339   const TypeAryPtr* top_y = y_type->isa_aryptr();
5340   if (top_x  == NULL || top_x->klass()  == NULL ||
5341       top_y == NULL || top_y->klass() == NULL) {
5342     // failed array check
5343     return false;
5344   }
5345 
5346   BasicType x_elem = x_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5347   BasicType y_elem = y_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5348   if (x_elem != T_INT || y_elem != T_INT) {
5349     return false;
5350   }
5351 
5352   // Set the original stack and the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
5353   // the bytecode that invokes BigInteger.multiplyToLen() if deoptimization happens
5354   // on the return from z array allocation in runtime.
5355   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
5356     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
5357 
5358     Node* x_start = array_element_address(x, intcon(0), x_elem);
5359     Node* y_start = array_element_address(y, intcon(0), y_elem);
5360     // 'x_start' points to x array + scaled xlen
5361     // 'y_start' points to y array + scaled ylen
5362 
5363     // Allocate the result array
5364     Node* zlen = _gvn.transform(new AddINode(xlen, ylen));
5365     ciKlass* klass = ciTypeArrayKlass::make(T_INT);
5366     Node* klass_node = makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(klass));
5367 
5368     IdealKit ideal(this);
5369 
5370 #define __ ideal.
5371      Node* one = __ ConI(1);
5372      Node* zero = __ ConI(0);
5373      IdealVariable need_alloc(ideal), z_alloc(ideal);  __ declarations_done();
5374      __ set(need_alloc, zero);
5375      __ set(z_alloc, z);
5376      __ if_then(z, BoolTest::eq, null()); {
5377        __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5378      } __ else_(); {
5379        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5380        sync_kit(ideal);
5381        Node *cast = new CastPPNode(z, TypePtr::NOTNULL);
5382        cast->init_req(0, control());
5383        _gvn.set_type(cast, cast->bottom_type());
5384        C->record_for_igvn(cast);
5385 
5386        Node* zlen_arg = load_array_length(cast);
5387        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5388        __ sync_kit(this);
5389        __ if_then(zlen_arg, BoolTest::lt, zlen); {
5390          __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5391        } __ end_if();
5392      } __ end_if();
5393 
5394      __ if_then(__ value(need_alloc), BoolTest::ne, zero); {
5395        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5396        sync_kit(ideal);
5397        Node * narr = new_array(klass_node, zlen, 1);
5398        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5399        __ sync_kit(this);
5400        __ set(z_alloc, narr);
5401      } __ end_if();
5402 
5403      sync_kit(ideal);
5404      z = __ value(z_alloc);
5405      // Can't use TypeAryPtr::INTS which uses Bottom offset.
5406      _gvn.set_type(z, TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass));
5407      // Final sync IdealKit and GraphKit.
5408      final_sync(ideal);
5409 #undef __
5410 
5411     Node* z_start = array_element_address(z, intcon(0), T_INT);
5412 
5413     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5414                                    OptoRuntime::multiplyToLen_Type(),
5415                                    stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5416                                    x_start, xlen, y_start, ylen, z_start, zlen);
5417   } // original reexecute is set back here
5418 
5419   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
5420   set_result(z);
5421   return true;
5422 }
5423 
5424 //-------------inline_squareToLen------------------------------------
5425 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_squareToLen() {
5426   assert(UseSquareToLenIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5427 
5428   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::squareToLen();
5429   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5430     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5431   }
5432   const char* stubName = "squareToLen";
5433 
5434   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "implSquareToLen has 4 parameters");
5435 
5436   Node* x    = argument(0);
5437   Node* len  = argument(1);
5438   Node* z    = argument(2);
5439   Node* zlen = argument(3);
5440 
5441   x = must_be_not_null(x, true);
5442   z = must_be_not_null(z, true);
5443 
5444   const Type* x_type = x->Value(&_gvn);
5445   const Type* z_type = z->Value(&_gvn);
5446   const TypeAryPtr* top_x = x_type->isa_aryptr();
5447   const TypeAryPtr* top_z = z_type->isa_aryptr();
5448   if (top_x  == NULL || top_x->klass()  == NULL ||
5449       top_z  == NULL || top_z->klass()  == NULL) {
5450     // failed array check
5451     return false;
5452   }
5453 
5454   BasicType x_elem = x_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5455   BasicType z_elem = z_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5456   if (x_elem != T_INT || z_elem != T_INT) {
5457     return false;
5458   }
5459 
5460 
5461   Node* x_start = array_element_address(x, intcon(0), x_elem);
5462   Node* z_start = array_element_address(z, intcon(0), z_elem);
5463 
5464   Node*  call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5465                                   OptoRuntime::squareToLen_Type(),
5466                                   stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5467                                   x_start, len, z_start, zlen);
5468 
5469   set_result(z);
5470   return true;
5471 }

5473 //-------------inline_mulAdd------------------------------------------
5474 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_mulAdd() {
5475   assert(UseMulAddIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5476 
5477   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::mulAdd();
5478   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5479     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5480   }
5481   const char* stubName = "mulAdd";
5482 
5483   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "mulAdd has 5 parameters");
5484 
5485   Node* out      = argument(0);
5486   Node* in       = argument(1);
5487   Node* offset   = argument(2);
5488   Node* len      = argument(3);
5489   Node* k        = argument(4);
5490 
5491   out = must_be_not_null(out, true);
5492 
5493   const Type* out_type = out->Value(&_gvn);
5494   const Type* in_type = in->Value(&_gvn);
5495   const TypeAryPtr* top_out = out_type->isa_aryptr();
5496   const TypeAryPtr* top_in = in_type->isa_aryptr();
5497   if (top_out  == NULL || top_out->klass()  == NULL ||
5498       top_in == NULL || top_in->klass() == NULL) {
5499     // failed array check
5500     return false;
5501   }
5502 
5503   BasicType out_elem = out_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5504   BasicType in_elem = in_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5505   if (out_elem != T_INT || in_elem != T_INT) {
5506     return false;
5507   }
5508 
5509   Node* outlen = load_array_length(out);
5510   Node* new_offset = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(outlen, offset));
5511   Node* out_start = array_element_address(out, intcon(0), out_elem);
5512   Node* in_start = array_element_address(in, intcon(0), in_elem);
5513 
5514   Node*  call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5515                                   OptoRuntime::mulAdd_Type(),
5516                                   stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5517                                   out_start,in_start, new_offset, len, k);
5518   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5519   set_result(result);
5520   return true;
5521 }

5526   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5527     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5528   }

5534

5539   Node* inv  = argument(4);
5540   Node* m    = argument(6);
5541

5543   const TypeAryPtr* top_a = a_type->isa_aryptr();
5544   const Type* b_type = b->Value(&_gvn);
5545   const TypeAryPtr* top_b = b_type->isa_aryptr();
5546   const Type* n_type = a->Value(&_gvn);
5547   const TypeAryPtr* top_n = n_type->isa_aryptr();
5548   const Type* m_type = a->Value(&_gvn);
5549   const TypeAryPtr* top_m = m_type->isa_aryptr();
5550   if (top_a  == NULL || top_a->klass()  == NULL ||
5551       top_b == NULL || top_b->klass()  == NULL ||
5552       top_n == NULL || top_n->klass()  == NULL ||

5559   BasicType b_elem = b_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();

5567   {

5569     Node* b_start = array_element_address(b, intcon(0), b_elem);
5570     Node* n_start = array_element_address(n, intcon(0), n_elem);
5571     Node* m_start = array_element_address(m, intcon(0), m_elem);
5572 
5573     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF,
5574                                    OptoRuntime::montgomeryMultiply_Type(),
5575                                    stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5576                                    a_start, b_start, n_start, len, inv, top(),
5577                                    m_start);

5638 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_bigIntegerShift(bool isRightShift) {
5639   address stubAddr = NULL;
5640   const char* stubName = NULL;
5641 
5642   stubAddr = isRightShift? StubRoutines::bigIntegerRightShift(): StubRoutines::bigIntegerLeftShift();
5643   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5644     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5645   }
5646 
5647   stubName = isRightShift? "bigIntegerRightShiftWorker" : "bigIntegerLeftShiftWorker";
5648 
5649   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "expected 5 arguments");
5650 
5651   Node* newArr = argument(0);
5652   Node* oldArr = argument(1);
5653   Node* newIdx = argument(2);
5654   Node* shiftCount = argument(3);
5655   Node* numIter = argument(4);
5656 
5657   const Type* newArr_type = newArr->Value(&_gvn);
5658   const TypeAryPtr* top_newArr = newArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5659   const Type* oldArr_type = oldArr->Value(&_gvn);
5660   const TypeAryPtr* top_oldArr = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5661   if (top_newArr == NULL || top_newArr->klass() == NULL || top_oldArr == NULL
5662       || top_oldArr->klass() == NULL) {
5663     return false;
5664   }
5665 
5666   BasicType newArr_elem = newArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5667   BasicType oldArr_elem = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5668   if (newArr_elem != T_INT || oldArr_elem != T_INT) {
5669     return false;
5670   }
5671 
5672   // Make the call
5673   {
5674     Node* newArr_start = array_element_address(newArr, intcon(0), newArr_elem);
5675     Node* oldArr_start = array_element_address(oldArr, intcon(0), oldArr_elem);
5676 
5677     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF,
5678                                    OptoRuntime::bigIntegerShift_Type(),
5679                                    stubAddr,
5680                                    stubName,
5681                                    TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5682                                    newArr_start,
5683                                    oldArr_start,
5684                                    newIdx,
5685                                    shiftCount,
5686                                    numIter);
5687   }
5688 
5689   return true;
5690 }

5697   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5698     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5699   }
5700   const char* stubName = "vectorizedMismatch";
5701   int size_l = callee()->signature()->size();
5702   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 8, "vectorizedMismatch has 6 parameters");
5703

5705   Node* aoffset = argument(1);
5706   Node* objb = argument(3);
5707   Node* boffset = argument(4);
