5737 /**
5738  * Calculate CRC32 for byte.
5739  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.update(int crc, int b)
5740  */
5741 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateCRC32() {
5742   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5743   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "update has 2 parameters");
5744   // no receiver since it is static method
5745   Node* crc  = argument(0); // type: int
5746   Node* b    = argument(1); // type: int
5747 
5748   /*
5749    *    int c = ~ crc;
5750    *    b = timesXtoThe32[(b ^ c) & 0xFF];
5751    *    b = b ^ (c >>> 8);
5752    *    crc = ~b;
5753    */
5754 
5755   Node* M1 = intcon(-1);
5756   crc = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, M1));
5757   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, b));
5758   result = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(result, intcon(0xFF)));
5759 
5760   Node* base = makecon(TypeRawPtr::make(StubRoutines::crc_table_addr()));
5761   Node* offset = _gvn.transform(new LShiftINode(result, intcon(0x2)));
5762   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, ConvI2X(offset));
5763   result = make_load(control(), adr, TypeInt::INT, T_INT, MemNode::unordered);
5764 
5765   crc = _gvn.transform(new URShiftINode(crc, intcon(8)));
5766   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, result));
5767   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(result, M1));
5768   set_result(result);
5769   return true;
5770 }
5771 
5772 /**
5773  * Calculate CRC32 for byte[] array.
5774  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateBytes(int crc, byte[] buf, int off, int len)
5775  */
5776 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesCRC32() {
5777   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5778   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5779   // no receiver since it is static method
5780   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5781   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5782   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5783   Node* length  = argument(3); // type: int
5784 
5785   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5786   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5787   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5788     // failed array check
5789     return false;
5790   }
5791 
5792   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5793   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5794   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5795     return false;
5796   }
5797 
5798   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5799   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5800   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5801 
5802   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
5803   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
5804 
5805   // Call the stub.
5806   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5807   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5808 
5809   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5810                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5811                                  crc, src_start, length);
5812   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5813   set_result(result);
5814   return true;
5815 }

5817 /**
5818  * Calculate CRC32 for ByteBuffer.
5819  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int len)
5820  */
5821 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateByteBufferCRC32() {
5822   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5823   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
5824   // no receiver since it is static method
5825   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5826   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
5827   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
5828   Node* length  = argument(4); // type: int
5829 
5830   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
5831   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
5832   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
5833 
5834   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5835   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
5836 
5837   // Call the stub.
5838   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5839   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5840 
5841   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5842                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5843                                  crc, src_start, length);
5844   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5845   set_result(result);
5846   return true;
5847 }

5850 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_table_from_crc32c_class(ciInstanceKlass *crc32c_class) {
5851   Node* table = load_field_from_object(NULL, "byteTable", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false, /*is_static*/ true, crc32c_class);
5852   assert (table != NULL, "wrong version of java.util.zip.CRC32C");
5853 
5854   return table;
5855 }

5957 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesAdler32() {

5959   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5960   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "Adler32 class must be loaded");
5961   // no receiver since it is static method
5962   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int

5964   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5965   Node* length  = argument(3); // type: int

5968   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5969   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5970     // failed array check

5972   }
5973 
5974   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5975   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5976   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5977     return false;
5978   }
5979 
5980   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5981   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5982 
5983   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
5984   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
5985 
5986   // Call the stub.
5987   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesAdler32();
5988   const char *stubName = "updateBytesAdler32";
5989 
5990   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesAdler32_Type(),
5991                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5992                                  crc, src_start, length);
5993   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5994   set_result(result);
5995   return true;
5996 }
5997 
5998 //------------------------------inline_updateByteBufferAdler32---------------
5999 //
6000 // Calculate Adler32 checksum for DirectByteBuffer.
6001 // int java.util.zip.Adler32.updateByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int len)
6002 //
6003 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateByteBufferAdler32() {
6004   assert(UseAdler32Intrinsics, "Adler32 Instrinsic support need"); // check if we actually need to check this flag or check a different one
6005   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
6006   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "Adler32 class must be loaded");
6007   // no receiver since it is static method
6008   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
6009   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
6010   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
6011   Node* length  = argument(4); // type: int
6012 
6013   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
6014   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
6015   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
6016 
6017   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
6018   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
6019 
6020   // Call the stub.
6021   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesAdler32();
6022   const char *stubName = "updateBytesAdler32";
6023 
6024   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesAdler32_Type(),
6025                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6026                                  crc, src_start, length);
6027 
6028   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6029   set_result(result);
6030   return true;
6031 }
6032 
6033 //----------------------------inline_reference_get----------------------------
6034 // public T java.lang.ref.Reference.get();
6035 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_reference_get() {
6036   const int referent_offset = java_lang_ref_Reference::referent_offset();
6037 
6038   // Get the argument:
6039   Node* reference_obj = null_check_receiver();
6040   if (stopped()) return true;
6041 
6042   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(reference_obj)->isa_instptr();
6043   assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6044   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6045   ciInstanceKlass* referenceKlass = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6046   ciField* field = referenceKlass->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make("referent"),
6047                                                      ciSymbol::make("Ljava/lang/Object;"),
6048                                                      false);
6049   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
6050 
6051   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(reference_obj, reference_obj, referent_offset);
6052   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
6053 
6054   ciInstanceKlass* klass = env()->Object_klass();
6055   const TypeOopPtr* object_type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass);
6056 
6057   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP | ON_WEAK_OOP_REF;
6058   Node* result = access_load_at(reference_obj, adr, adr_type, object_type, T_OBJECT, decorators);
6059   // Add memory barrier to prevent commoning reads from this field
6060   // across safepoint since GC can change its value.
6061   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
6062 
6063   set_result(result);
6064   return true;
6065 }
6066 
6067 
6068 Node * LibraryCallKit::load_field_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
6069                                               bool is_exact=true, bool is_static=false,
6070                                               ciInstanceKlass * fromKls=NULL) {
6071   if (fromKls == NULL) {
6072     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
6073     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6074     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6075     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
6076     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6077   } else {
6078     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
6079   }
6080   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
6081                                               ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
6082                                               is_static);
6083 
6084   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
6085   if (field == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6086 
6087   if (is_static) {
6088     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
6089     fromObj = makecon(tip);
6090   }
6091 
6092   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
6093 
6094   // Compute address and memory type.
6095   int offset  = field->offset_in_bytes();
6096   bool is_vol = field->is_volatile();
6097   ciType* field_klass = field->type();
6098   assert(field_klass->is_loaded(), "should be loaded");
6099   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
6100   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
6101   BasicType bt = field->layout_type();
6102 
6103   // Build the resultant type of the load
6104   const Type *type;
6105   if (bt == T_OBJECT) {
6106     type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(field_klass->as_klass());
6107   } else {
6108     type = Type::get_const_basic_type(bt);
6109   }
6110 
6111   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP;
6112 
6113   if (is_vol) {
6114     decorators |= MO_SEQ_CST;
6115   }
6116 
6117   return access_load_at(fromObj, adr, adr_type, type, bt, decorators);
6118 }
6119 
6120 Node * LibraryCallKit::field_address_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
6121                                                  bool is_exact = true, bool is_static = false,
6122                                                  ciInstanceKlass * fromKls = NULL) {
6123   if (fromKls == NULL) {
6124     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
6125     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6126     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6127     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
6128     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6129   }
6130   else {
6131     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
6132   }
6133   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
6134     ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
6135     is_static);
6136 
6137   assert(field != NULL, "undefined field");
6138   assert(!field->is_volatile(), "not defined for volatile fields");
6139 
6140   if (is_static) {
6141     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
6142     fromObj = makecon(tip);
6143   }
6144 
6145   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
6146 
6147   // Compute address and memory type.
6148   int offset = field->offset_in_bytes();
6149   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
6150 
6151   return adr;
6152 }

6154 //------------------------------inline_aescrypt_Block-----------------------
6155 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_aescrypt_Block(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6156   address stubAddr = NULL;
6157   const char *stubName;
6158   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6159 
6160   switch(id) {
6161   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_encryptBlock:
6162     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_encryptBlock();
6163     stubName = "aescrypt_encryptBlock";
6164     break;
6165   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_decryptBlock:
6166     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_decryptBlock();
6167     stubName = "aescrypt_decryptBlock";
6168     break;
6169   default:
6170     break;
6171   }
6172   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6173 
6174   Node* aescrypt_object = argument(0);
6175   Node* src             = argument(1);
6176   Node* src_offset      = argument(2);
6177   Node* dest            = argument(3);
6178   Node* dest_offset     = argument(4);
6179 
6180   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6181   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
6182 
6183   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6184   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6185   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6186   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6187   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6188   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6189 
6190   // for the quick and dirty code we will skip all the checks.
6191   // we are just trying to get the call to be generated.
6192   Node* src_start  = src;
6193   Node* dest_start = dest;
6194   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6195     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6196     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
6197     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6198   }
6199 
6200   // now need to get the start of its expanded key array
6201   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6202   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6203   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6204 
6205   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6206     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
6207     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
6208     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6209     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
6210 
6211     // Call the stub.
6212     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
6213                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6214                       src_start, dest_start, k_start, original_k_start);
6215   } else {
6216     // Call the stub.
6217     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
6218                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6219                       src_start, dest_start, k_start);
6220   }
6221 
6222   return true;
6223 }
6224 
6225 //------------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt-----------------------
6226 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6227   address stubAddr = NULL;
6228   const char *stubName = NULL;
6229 
6230   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6231 
6232   switch(id) {
6233   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt:
6234     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt();
6235     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt";
6236     break;
6237   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt:
6238     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt();
6239     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt";
6240     break;
6241   default:
6242     break;
6243   }
6244   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6245 
6246   Node* cipherBlockChaining_object = argument(0);
6247   Node* src                        = argument(1);
6248   Node* src_offset                 = argument(2);
6249   Node* len                        = argument(3);
6250   Node* dest                       = argument(4);
6251   Node* dest_offset                = argument(5);
6252 
6253   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
6254   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, false);
6255 
6256   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6257   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6258   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6259   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6260   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6261   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL
6262           &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6263 
6264   // checks are the responsibility of the caller
6265   Node* src_start  = src;
6266   Node* dest_start = dest;
6267   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6268     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6269     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
6270     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6271   }
6272 
6273   // if we are in this set of code, we "know" the embeddedCipher is an AESCrypt object
6274   // (because of the predicated logic executed earlier).
6275   // so we cast it here safely.
6276   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6277 
6278   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6279   if (embeddedCipherObj == NULL) return false;
6280 
6281   // cast it to what we know it will be at runtime
6282   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(cipherBlockChaining_object)->isa_instptr();
6283   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBC obj is null");
6284   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBC obj is not loaded");
6285   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6286   assert(klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6287 
6288   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6289   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6290   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6291   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6292   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6293 
6294   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6295   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6296   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6297 
6298   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
6299   Node* objRvec = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "r", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6300   if (objRvec == NULL) return false;
6301   Node* r_start = array_element_address(objRvec, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6302 
6303   Node* cbcCrypt;
6304   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6305     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
6306     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
6307     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6308     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
6309 
6310     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, src_len and original_k_start
6311     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6312                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
6313                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6314                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len, original_k_start);
6315   } else {
6316     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6317     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6318                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
6319                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6320                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len);
6321   }
6322 
6323   // return cipher length (int)
6324   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(cbcCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6325   set_result(retvalue);
6326   return true;
6327 }

6466   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6467   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6468   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6469   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6470   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6471   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6472   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6473   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6474   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
6475   Node* obj_counter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "counter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6476   if (obj_counter == NULL) return false;
6477   Node* cnt_start = array_element_address(obj_counter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6478 
6479   Node* saved_encCounter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "encryptedCounter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6480   if (saved_encCounter == NULL) return false;
6481   Node* saved_encCounter_start = array_element_address(saved_encCounter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6482   Node* used = field_address_from_object(counterMode_object, "used", "I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6483 
6484   Node* ctrCrypt;
6485   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6486     // no SPARC version for AES/CTR intrinsics now.
6487     return false;
6488   }
6489   // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6490   ctrCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6491                                OptoRuntime::counterMode_aescrypt_Type(),
6492                                stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6493                                src_start, dest_start, k_start, cnt_start, len, saved_encCounter_start, used);
6494 
6495   // return cipher length (int)
6496   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(ctrCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6497   set_result(retvalue);
6498   return true;
6499 }
6500 
6501 //------------------------------get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6502 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6503 #if defined(PPC64) || defined(S390)
6504   // MixColumns for decryption can be reduced by preprocessing MixColumns with round keys.
6505   // Intel's extention is based on this optimization and AESCrypt generates round keys by preprocessing MixColumns.
6506   // However, ppc64 vncipher processes MixColumns and requires the same round keys with encryption.
6507   // The ppc64 stubs of encryption and decryption use the same round keys (sessionK[0]).
6508   Node* objSessionK = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "sessionK", "[[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6509   assert (objSessionK != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6510   if (objSessionK == NULL) {
6511     return (Node *) NULL;
6512   }
6513   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_array_element(control(), objSessionK, intcon(0), TypeAryPtr::OOPS);
6514 #else
6515   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "K", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6516 #endif // PPC64
6517   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6518   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6519 
6520   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the K array
6521   Node* k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_INT);
6522   return k_start;
6523 }
6524 
6525 //------------------------------get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6526 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6527   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "lastKey", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6528   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6529   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6530 
6531   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the lastKey array
6532   Node* original_k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6533   return original_k_start;
6534 }
6535 
6536 //----------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6537 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6538 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6539 // for encryption:
6540 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6541 // for decryption:
6542 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6543 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6544 //
6545 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {
6546   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6547   Node* objCBC = argument(0);
6548 
6549   Node* src = argument(1);
6550   Node* dest = argument(4);
6551 
6552   // Load embeddedCipher field of CipherBlockChaining object.
6553   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objCBC, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6554 
6555   // get AESCrypt klass for instanceOf check
6556   // AESCrypt might not be loaded yet if some other SymmetricCipher got us to this compile point
6557   // will have same classloader as CipherBlockChaining object
6558   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(objCBC)->isa_instptr();
6559   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBCobj is null");
6560   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBCobj is not loaded");
6561 
6562   // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the AESCrypt class
6563   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6564   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6565     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6566     Node* ctrl = control();
6567     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6568     return ctrl;
6569   }
6570 
6571   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6572   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
6573 
6574   // Resolve oops to stable for CmpP below.
6575   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6576 
6577   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6578   Node* cmp_instof  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6579   Node* bool_instof  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
6580 
6581   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6582 
6583   // for encryption, we are done
6584   if (!decrypting)
6585     return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6586 
6587   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6588   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6589   // see the original java code for why.
6590   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6591   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6592 
6593   Node* cmp_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(src, dest));
6594   Node* bool_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_src_dest, BoolTest::eq));
6595   Node* src_dest_conjoint = generate_guard(bool_src_dest, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6596   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6597 
6598   record_for_igvn(region);
6599   return _gvn.transform(region);
6600 }

6602 //----------------------------inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6603 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6604 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6605 // for encryption:
6606 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6607 // for decryption:
6608 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6609 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6610 //
6611 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {
6612   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.

6614

6616   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objECB, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6617

6620   // will have same classloader as ElectronicCodeBook object

6622   assert(tinst != NULL, "ECBobj is null");
6623   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "ECBobj is not loaded");
6624 
6625   // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the AESCrypt class
6626   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6627   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6628     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6629     Node* ctrl = control();
6630     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6631     return ctrl;
6632   }
6633   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6634 
6635   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6636   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6637   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));

6640 
6641   // for encryption, we are done
6642   if (!decrypting)
6643     return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6644 
6645   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6646   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6647   // see the original java code for why.
6648   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6649   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6650   Node* src = argument(1);
6651   Node* dest = argument(4);
6652   Node* cmp_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(src, dest));

6655   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6656 
6657   record_for_igvn(region);
6658   return _gvn.transform(region);
6659 }

6703 //------------------------------inline_ghash_processBlocks
6704 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_ghash_processBlocks() {
6705   address stubAddr;
6706   const char *stubName;
6707   assert(UseGHASHIntrinsics, "need GHASH intrinsics support");
6708 
6709   stubAddr = StubRoutines::ghash_processBlocks();
6710   stubName = "ghash_processBlocks";
6711 
6712   Node* data           = argument(0);
6713   Node* offset         = argument(1);
6714   Node* len            = argument(2);
6715   Node* state          = argument(3);
6716   Node* subkeyH        = argument(4);
6717 
6718   state = must_be_not_null(state, true);
6719   subkeyH = must_be_not_null(subkeyH, true);
6720   data = must_be_not_null(data, true);
6721 
6722   Node* state_start  = array_element_address(state, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6723   assert(state_start, "state is NULL");
6724   Node* subkeyH_start  = array_element_address(subkeyH, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6725   assert(subkeyH_start, "subkeyH is NULL");
6726   Node* data_start  = array_element_address(data, offset, T_BYTE);
6727   assert(data_start, "data is NULL");
6728 
6729   Node* ghash = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6730                                   OptoRuntime::ghash_processBlocks_Type(),
6731                                   stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6732                                   state_start, subkeyH_start, data_start, len);
6733   return true;
6734 }

6768 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompress-----------------------
6769 //
6770 // Calculate SHA (i.e., SHA-1) for single-block byte[] array.
6771 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6772 //
6773 // Calculate SHA2 (i.e., SHA-244 or SHA-256) for single-block byte[] array.
6774 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA2.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6775 //
6776 // Calculate SHA5 (i.e., SHA-384 or SHA-512) for single-block byte[] array.
6777 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA5.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6778 //
6779 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompress(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6780   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "sha_implCompress has 2 parameters");
6781 
6782   Node* sha_obj = argument(0);
6783   Node* src     = argument(1); // type oop
6784   Node* ofs     = argument(2); // type int
6785 
6786   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6787   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6788   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6789     // failed array check
6790     return false;
6791   }
6792   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6793   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6794   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6795     return false;
6796   }
6797   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6798   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6799   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6800   Node* state = NULL;
6801   address stubAddr;
6802   const char *stubName;
6803 
6804   switch(id) {
6805   case vmIntrinsics::_sha_implCompress:
6806     assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics, "need SHA1 instruction support");
6807     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6808     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompress();
6809     stubName = "sha1_implCompress";
6810     break;
6811   case vmIntrinsics::_sha2_implCompress:
6812     assert(UseSHA256Intrinsics, "need SHA256 instruction support");
6813     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6814     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompress();
6815     stubName = "sha256_implCompress";
6816     break;
6817   case vmIntrinsics::_sha5_implCompress:
6818     assert(UseSHA512Intrinsics, "need SHA512 instruction support");
6819     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6820     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompress();
6821     stubName = "sha512_implCompress";
6822     break;
6823   default:
6824     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
6825     return false;
6826   }
6827   if (state == NULL) return false;
6828 
6829   assert(stubAddr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6830   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6831 
6832   // Call the stub.
6833   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::sha_implCompress_Type(),
6834                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6835                                  src_start, state);
6836 
6837   return true;
6838 }
6839 
6840 //------------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB-----------------------
6841 //
6842 // Calculate SHA/SHA2/SHA5 for multi-block byte[] array.
6843 // int com.sun.security.provider.DigestBase.implCompressMultiBlock(byte[] b, int ofs, int limit)
6844 //
6845 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB(int predicate) {
6846   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
6847          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
6848   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
6849   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "digestBase_implCompressMB has 3 parameters");
6850 
6851   Node* digestBase_obj = argument(0); // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6852   Node* src            = argument(1); // byte[] array
6853   Node* ofs            = argument(2); // type int
6854   Node* limit          = argument(3); // type int
6855 
6856   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6857   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6858   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6859     // failed array check
6860     return false;
6861   }
6862   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6863   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6864   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6865     return false;
6866   }
6867   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6868   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
6869   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6870 
6871   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
6872   const char* stub_name = NULL;
6873   address     stub_addr = NULL;
6874   bool        long_state = false;
6875 
6876   switch (predicate) {
6877   case 0:
6878     if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_sha_implCompress)) {
6879       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
6880       stub_name = "sha1_implCompressMB";
6881       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompressMB();
6882     }
6883     break;
6884   case 1:
6885     if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_sha2_implCompress)) {
6886       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
6887       stub_name = "sha256_implCompressMB";
6888       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompressMB();
6889     }
6890     break;
6891   case 2:
6892     if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_sha5_implCompress)) {
6893       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
6894       stub_name = "sha512_implCompressMB";
6895       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompressMB();
6896       long_state = true;
6897     }
6898     break;
6899   default:
6900     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
6901   }
6902   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
6903     assert(stub_addr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6904     if (stub_addr == NULL) return false;
6905 
6906     // get DigestBase klass to lookup for SHA klass
6907     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBase_obj)->isa_instptr();
6908     assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBase_obj is not instance???");
6909     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
6910 
6911     ciKlass* klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
6912     assert(klass_SHA->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6913     ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
6914     return inline_sha_implCompressMB(digestBase_obj, instklass_SHA, long_state, stub_addr, stub_name, src_start, ofs, limit);
6915   }
6916   return false;
6917 }
6918 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompressMB-----------------------
6919 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompressMB(Node* digestBase_obj, ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA,
6920                                                bool long_state, address stubAddr, const char *stubName,
6921                                                Node* src_start, Node* ofs, Node* limit) {
6922   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA);
6923   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6924   Node* sha_obj = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), digestBase_obj, xtype);
6925   sha_obj = _gvn.transform(sha_obj);
6926 
6927   Node* state;
6928   if (long_state) {
6929     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6930   } else {
6931     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6932   }
6933   if (state == NULL) return false;
6934 
6935   // Call the stub.
6936   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6937                                  OptoRuntime::digestBase_implCompressMB_Type(),
6938                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6939                                  src_start, state, ofs, limit);
6940   // return ofs (int)
6941   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6942   set_result(result);
6943 
6944   return true;
6945 }
6946 
6947 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha_object-----------------------
6948 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha_object(Node *sha_object) {
6949   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6950   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA/SHA2");
6951   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6952 
6953   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6954   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_INT);
6955   return state;
6956 }
6957 
6958 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha5_object-----------------------
6959 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha5_object(Node *sha_object) {
6960   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[J", /*is_exact*/ false);
6961   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA5");
6962   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6963 
6964   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6965   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6966   return state;
6967 }
6968 
6969 //----------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate----------------------------
6970 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6971 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6972 //    if (digestBaseObj instanceof SHA/SHA2/SHA5) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6973 //
6974 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate(int predicate) {
6975   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
6976          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
6977   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
6978 
6979   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6980   Node* digestBaseObj = argument(0);
6981 
6982   // get DigestBase klass for instanceOf check
6983   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBaseObj)->isa_instptr();
6984   assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBaseObj is null");
6985   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
6986 
6987   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
6988   switch (predicate) {
6989   case 0:
6990     if (UseSHA1Intrinsics) {
6991       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA class
6992       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
6993     }
6994     break;
6995   case 1:
6996     if (UseSHA256Intrinsics) {
6997       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA2 class
6998       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
6999     }
7000     break;
7001   case 2:
7002     if (UseSHA512Intrinsics) {
7003       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA5 class
7004       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
7005     }
7006     break;
7007   default:
7008     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
7009   }
7010 
7011   ciKlass* klass_SHA = NULL;
7012   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
7013     klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
7014   }
7015   if ((klass_SHA == NULL) || !klass_SHA->is_loaded()) {
7016     // if none of SHA/SHA2/SHA5 is loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
7017     Node* ctrl = control();
7018     set_control(top()); // no intrinsic path
7019     return ctrl;
7020   }
7021   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
7022 
7023   Node* instofSHA = gen_instanceof(digestBaseObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA)));
7024   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instofSHA, intcon(1)));
7025   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
7026   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
7027 
7028   return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
7029 }
7030 
7031 //-------------inline_fma-----------------------------------
7032 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fma(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7033   Node *a = NULL;
7034   Node *b = NULL;
7035   Node *c = NULL;
7036   Node* result = NULL;
7037   switch (id) {
7038   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaD:
7039     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 6, "fma has 3 parameters of size 2 each.");
7040     // no receiver since it is static method
7041     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
7042     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
7043     c = round_double_node(argument(4));
7044     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaDNode(control(), a, b, c));
7045     break;
7046   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaF:
7047     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "fma has 3 parameters of size 1 each.");
7048     a = argument(0);
7049     b = argument(1);
7050     c = argument(2);
7051     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaFNode(control(), a, b, c));
7052     break;
7053   default:
7054     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
7055   }
7056   set_result(result);
7057   return true;
7058 }
7059 
7060 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_character_compare(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7061   // argument(0) is receiver
7062   Node* codePoint = argument(1);
7063   Node* n = NULL;
7064 
7065   switch (id) {
7066     case vmIntrinsics::_isDigit :
7067       n = new DigitNode(control(), codePoint);
7068       break;
7069     case vmIntrinsics::_isLowerCase :
7070       n = new LowerCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
7071       break;
7072     case vmIntrinsics::_isUpperCase :
7073       n = new UpperCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
7074       break;
7075     case vmIntrinsics::_isWhitespace :
7076       n = new WhitespaceNode(control(), codePoint);
7077       break;
7078     default:
7079       fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
7080   }
7081 
7082   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
7083   return true;
7084 }
7085 
7086 //------------------------------inline_fp_min_max------------------------------
7087 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fp_min_max(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7088 /* DISABLED BECAUSE METHOD DATA ISN'T COLLECTED PER CALL-SITE, SEE JDK-8015416.
7089 
7090   // The intrinsic should be used only when the API branches aren't predictable,
7091   // the last one performing the most important comparison. The following heuristic
7092   // uses the branch statistics to eventually bail out if necessary.
7093 
7094   ciMethodData *md = callee()->method_data();
7095 
7096   if ( md != NULL && md->is_mature() && md->invocation_count() > 0 ) {
7097     ciCallProfile cp = caller()->call_profile_at_bci(bci());
7098 
7099     if ( ((double)cp.count()) / ((double)md->invocation_count()) < 0.8 ) {
7100       // Bail out if the call-site didn't contribute enough to the statistics.
7101       return false;
7102     }
7103 
7104     uint taken = 0, not_taken = 0;
7105 
7106     for (ciProfileData *p = md->first_data(); md->is_valid(p); p = md->next_data(p)) {
7107       if (p->is_BranchData()) {
7108         taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->taken();
7109         not_taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->not_taken();
7110       }
7111     }
7112 
7113     double balance = (((double)taken) - ((double)not_taken)) / ((double)md->invocation_count());
7114     balance = balance < 0 ? -balance : balance;
7115     if ( balance > 0.2 ) {
7116       // Bail out if the most important branch is predictable enough.
7117       return false;
7118     }
7119   }
7120 */
7121 
7122   Node *a = NULL;
7123   Node *b = NULL;
7124   Node *n = NULL;
7125   switch (id) {
7126   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:
7127   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:
7128     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "minF/maxF has 2 parameters of size 1 each.");
7129     a = argument(0);
7130     b = argument(1);
7131     break;
7132   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:
7133   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:
7134     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "minD/maxD has 2 parameters of size 2 each.");
7135     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
7136     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
7137     break;
7138   default:
7139     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
7140     break;
7141   }
7142   switch (id) {
7143   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:  n = new MaxFNode(a, b);  break;
7144   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:  n = new MinFNode(a, b);  break;
7145   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:  n = new MaxDNode(a, b);  break;
7146   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:  n = new MinDNode(a, b);  break;
7147   default:  fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
7148   }
7149   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
7150   return true;
7151 }
7152 
7153 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_profileBoolean() {
7154   Node* counts = argument(1);
7155   const TypeAryPtr* ary = NULL;
7156   ciArray* aobj = NULL;
7157   if (counts->is_Con()
7158       && (ary = counts->bottom_type()->isa_aryptr()) != NULL
7159       && (aobj = ary->const_oop()->as_array()) != NULL
7160       && (aobj->length() == 2)) {
7161     // Profile is int[2] where [0] and [1] correspond to false and true value occurrences respectively.
7162     jint false_cnt = aobj->element_value(0).as_int();
7163     jint  true_cnt = aobj->element_value(1).as_int();
7164 
7165     if (C->log() != NULL) {
7166       C->log()->elem("observe source='profileBoolean' false='%d' true='%d'",
7167                      false_cnt, true_cnt);
7168     }
7169 
7170     if (false_cnt + true_cnt == 0) {
7171       // According to profile, never executed.
7172       uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
7173                           Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
7174       return true;
7175     }
7176 
7177     // result is a boolean (0 or 1) and its profile (false_cnt & true_cnt)
7178     // is a number of each value occurrences.
7179     Node* result = argument(0);
7180     if (false_cnt == 0 || true_cnt == 0) {
7181       // According to profile, one value has been never seen.
7182       int expected_val = (false_cnt == 0) ? 1 : 0;
7183 
7184       Node* cmp  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(result, intcon(expected_val)));
7185       Node* test = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp, BoolTest::eq));
7186 
7187       IfNode* check = create_and_map_if(control(), test, PROB_ALWAYS, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
7188       Node* fast_path = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(check));
7189       Node* slow_path = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(check));
7190 
7191       { // Slow path: uncommon trap for never seen value and then reexecute
7192         // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() to bump the count, so JIT knows
7193         // the value has been seen at least once.
7194         PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
7195         PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
7196         jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
7197 
7198         set_control(slow_path);
7199         set_i_o(i_o());
7200 
7201         uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
7202                             Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
7203       }
7204       // The guard for never seen value enables sharpening of the result and
7205       // returning a constant. It allows to eliminate branches on the same value
7206       // later on.
7207       set_control(fast_path);
7208       result = intcon(expected_val);
7209     }
7210     // Stop profiling.
7211     // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() has profiling logic in its bytecode.
7212     // By replacing method body with profile data (represented as ProfileBooleanNode
7213     // on IR level) we effectively disable profiling.
7214     // It enables full speed execution once optimized code is generated.
7215     Node* profile = _gvn.transform(new ProfileBooleanNode(result, false_cnt, true_cnt));
7216     C->record_for_igvn(profile);
7217     set_result(profile);
7218     return true;
7219   } else {
7220     // Continue profiling.
7221     // Profile data isn't available at the moment. So, execute method's bytecode version.
7222     // Usually, when GWT LambdaForms are profiled it means that a stand-alone nmethod
7223     // is compiled and counters aren't available since corresponding MethodHandle
7224     // isn't a compile-time constant.
7225     return false;
7226   }
7227 }
7228 
7229 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_isCompileConstant() {
7230   Node* n = argument(0);
7231   set_result(n->is_Con() ? intcon(1) : intcon(0));
7232   return true;
7233 }
